          )

            (bn1): SyncBatchNorm(48, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)
            (relu): ReLU(inplace=True)

              )
              (2): Conv2d(256, 128, kernel_size=(1, 1), stride=(1, 1))

          )
        )

    )
